function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }

if (!is_file('includes/edition.ini')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/edition.ini');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('includes/edition.ini')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/edition.ini');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/edition.ini') != '2a4ea0751edf7cb70d959e8d28c6d355cb5f40ee') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/edition.ini');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/edition.ini', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/edition.ini');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/edition.ini') !== '2a4ea0751edf7cb70d959e8d28c6d355cb5f40ee') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/edition.ini') !== 'ece6cd1accd1a5fa739a66d1d08917d11b476961') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/edition.ini');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/edition.ini');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/edition.ini')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/edition.ini', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/edition.ini') !== '2a4ea0751edf7cb70d959e8d28c6d355cb5f40ee') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/edition.ini');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '85c94dd8a40952b7cdbc5dcca8b8ba816e3deb1a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '85c94dd8a40952b7cdbc5dcca8b8ba816e3deb1a') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'f1fa968e282e68d2b72e48cc118f91ed5ed1bcf1') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '85c94dd8a40952b7cdbc5dcca8b8ba816e3deb1a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '605337f88fe510f8215c9ed6d0416e0f29918aa6') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '605337f88fe510f8215c9ed6d0416e0f29918aa6') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '94678275e3a51654c5ffaeaa9ebf06b42c57f85f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '605337f88fe510f8215c9ed6d0416e0f29918aa6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '7df5e324e9320b8daad490cf036470b4ae97bbc6') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== 'e10e340bd9b5487f43ec494a0cf4892cb7aaa7cc') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html') !== '7df5e324e9320b8daad490cf036470b4ae97bbc6') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/acknowledgements.html');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('.version.php', "<?php // Revision 822\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('.version.php')) !== '<?php // Revision 822') err('Could not write to .version.php!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
